            // Redirect script to /logged-out
            if (location.pathname === '/' && localStorage.postLogoutRedirect) {
                location.replace(localStorage.postLogoutRedirect);
                localStorage.removeItem('postLogoutRedirect');
            }
        </script>
        <script>
            // Redirect script /resource/slug > /no-access > /preview/?resource=slug
            if (location.pathname.replace(/\/+$/, '') === '/no-access') {
                var r = document.referrer;
                if (r && r.indexOf(location.origin + '/resource/') === 0) {
                    var m = r.match(/\/resource\/([^\/?#]+)/);
                    if (m) {
                        location.replace('/preview/?resource=' + m[1]);
                    }
                }
            }
        </script>

        <!-- Plausible -->
        <script>
            window.plausible = window.plausible || function() {
                (window.plausible.q = window.plausible.q || []).push(arguments)
            }
        </script>
        <script defer data-domain="osmo.supply" src="https://plausible.io/js/script.outbound-links.pageview-props.revenue.tagged-events.js"></script>
        <script>
            Outseta.on('signup', (account) => {
                if (typeof plausible !== 'function')
                    return;

                const sub = account?.LatestSubscription || {};
                const planName = sub?.Plan?.Name || '';
                const billingTermMap = {
                    1: 'Monthly',
                    3: 'Quarterly',
                    12: 'Yearly'
                };
                const billingTerm = billingTermMap[sub?.BillingRenewalTerm] || '';

                let product = planName;
                if (planName === 'Subscription' || planName === 'Subscription Team') {
                    product = `${planName} ${billingTerm}`;
                }

                const amount = Number(sub?.Rate ?? 0);
                const currency = 'EUR';

                const customer_type = account?.TaxId ? 'Business' : 'Private';
                const email = account?.PersonAccount?.[0]?.Person?.Email || '';

                const props = {
                    product,
                    customer_type,
                    email
                };

                plausible('Transaction', {
                    revenue: {
                        currency,
                        amount
                    },
                    props
                });
            }
            );
        </script>
